***эвакуировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:эвакуировать.html>эвакуи́ровать</a> (11400)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">evakuieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эвакуировать.html>эвакуи́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">evakuírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to evacuate</li>
<li>to tow away (a car)</li></ol>

***эдельвейс.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:эдельвейс.html>эдельве́йс</a> (23495)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Edelweiß</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">edel</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weiß</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эдельвейс.html>эдельве́йс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">edɛlʹvɛ́js, edɛlʹvéjs</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эдельвейс.html>эдельве́йса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эдельвейс.html>эдельве́йсы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эдельвейс.html>эдельве́йсов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>edelweiss (a European perennial alpine plant)</li></ol>

***экваториальный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экваториальный.html>экваториа́льный</a> (28545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">équatorial</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***экзаменатор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзаменатор.html>экзамена́тор</a> (17074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мен</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ekzámen</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́тор</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">э́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">é-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>what a ...</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>An alternative shorter nominative feminine singular <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">э́ка</span> can occur in the expressions <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">э́ка <a href = vnd.unilang:важность.html>ва́жность</a>, эка <a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беда́</a>, эка <a href = vnd.unilang:невидаль.html>не́видаль</a></span> (the normal form <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экий.html>эка́я</a></span> can also occur here).
